<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>iCAD Reports Financial Results for First Quarter Ended March&nbsp;31, 2022 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Company to host conference call and webcast today at 4:30 PM ET </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>NASHUA, N.H. &#150; May</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;11, 2022 &#150;</B> iCAD, Inc. (NASDAQ: ICAD),&nbsp;a global medical technology leader providing innovative
cancer detection and therapy solutions, today reported its financial and operating results for the three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Highlights:
</B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Commercial reorganization shows early success leading to a ProFound AI<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> enterprise agreement at a world-renowned academic research institution with multiple locations throughout the U.S. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Profound AI<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Risk clinical research progresses, with new
data to be presented at both the International Workshop on Breast Imaging (IWBI) and the European Congress of Radiology (ECR) in Q2 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GLIOX trial examining use of Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> intraoperative
radiation therapy (IORT) for recurrent glioblastoma (GBM) has accelerated with additional patients treated, and customers globally continue to expand use of Xoft electronic brachytherapy (eBx) for the treatment of multiple tumor types, including
rectal, head and neck, and various types of brain cancers </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Launched a new webinar series, &#147;ProFound Insights, ProFound Impact,&#148; which will highlight compelling
customer success stories, such as Kettering Health in Ohio and Wake Radiology in North Carolina </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We are currently at an important
inflection point that offers significant potential across both sides of our business,&#148; said Stacey Stevens, President and CEO of iCAD, Inc. &#147;With a robust portfolio of world-leading, differentiated solutions in large, under-penetrated
markets in the detection segment, and the expansion of Xoft in promising applications such as the treatment of brain tumors in the cancer therapy segment, iCAD is well positioned for sustained growth.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our results this quarter were achieved through solid execution of our strategic plan, which has laid the groundwork for continued success this year. We
will continue to leverage the strength of our robust portfolio of powerful solutions and expand access to our innovative technologies via aggressively targeting broader market opportunities and offering more flexible ways for our technologies to
meet customer needs,&#148; continued Stevens. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We remain optimistic as we look ahead, as we believe we now have a stronger commercial infrastructure
in place and a solid and growing pipeline to ensure the trajectory we are on will continue to position the organization for success and bring our leading portfolio of innovative solutions into the hands of more clinicians worldwide. I believe that
we have the right plans and the right team in place to successfully execute our strategic vision and elevate the Company and our technologies to new heights,&#148; Stevens added. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>First Quarter 2022 Financial Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total Detection and
Therapy revenue for the first quarter of 2022 was $7.5&nbsp;million, a decrease of $1.1&nbsp;million, or 13.0%, as compared to the first quarter of 2022, reflecting an 17.9% decrease in product revenue, and a 4.0% decrease in service and supplies
revenue. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In $000&#146;s </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue: Cancer detection revenue for the first quarter of 2022, which includes the Company&#146;s
mammography and breast density products, and the associated service and supplies revenue, decreased by approximately $0.2&nbsp;million, or 3.5%, to $5.5&nbsp;million, as compared to the first quarter of 2021. Therapy revenue for the first quarter of
2022, which includes Xoft<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> eBx<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> System<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> sales, as well as the associated
service and supplies revenue, decreased by $0.9&nbsp;million, or 31.6%, to $2.0&nbsp;million, as compared to the first quarter of 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In $000&#146;s

quarter of 2022 was ($3.5) million, or ($0.14) per diluted share, as compared to a net loss of ($1.6) million, or ($0.07) per diluted share, for the first quarter of 2021. </P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures as defined by SEC Regulation G. The GAAP financial measures most directly comparable to each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure used or discussed,
and a reconciliation of the differences between each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure and the comparable GAAP financial measure, are included in this press release after the condensed consolidated financial
statements. When analyzing the Company&#146;s operating performance, investors should not consider these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures as a substitute for the comparable financial measures prepared in accordance with
GAAP. The Company&#146;s quarterly news releases containing such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> reconciliations can be found on the Investors section of the Company&#146;s website at www.icadmed.com. </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to Comparable GAAP
Measures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company reports its financial results in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles, or GAAP. However,
management believes that in order to understand the Company&#146;s short-term and long-term financial and operational trends, investors may wish to consider the impact of certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> or <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items, when used as a supplement to financial performance measures in accordance with GAAP. These items result from facts and circumstances that vary in frequency and/or impact on continuing
operations. Management also uses results of operations before such items to evaluate the operating performance of the Company and compare it against past periods, make operating decisions, and serve as a basis for strategic planning. These <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide management with additional means to understand and evaluate the operating results and trends in the Company&#146;s ongoing business by eliminating certain <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses and other items that management believes might otherwise make comparisons of the Company&#146;s ongoing business with prior periods more difficult, obscure trends in ongoing operations or reduce
management&#146;s ability to make useful forecasts. Management believes that these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide additional means of evaluating period-over-period operating performance. In addition,
management understands that some investors and financial analysts find this information helpful in analyzing the Company&#146;s financial and operational performance and comparing this performance to its peers and competitors. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management defines <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA&#148; as the sum of GAAP Net Loss before provisions for interest
expense, other income, stock-based compensation expense, depreciation and amortization, tax expense, severance, gain on sale of assets, loss on disposal of assets, acquisition and litigation related expenses. Management considers this <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to be an indicator of the Company&#146;s operational strength and performance of its business and a good measure of its historical operating trends, in particular the extent to which
ongoing operations impact the Company&#146;s overall financial performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures do
not replace the presentation of the Company&#146;s GAAP financial results and should only be used as a supplement to, not as a substitute for, the Company&#146;s financial results presented in accordance with GAAP. The Company has provided a
reconciliation of each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure used in its financial reporting and investor presentations to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management excludes each of the items identified below from the applicable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure referenced above
for the reasons set forth with respect to that excluded item: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Interest expense: The Company excludes interest expense which includes interest from debt facility agreements and
interest on capital leases from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA calculation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Stock-based compensation expense: excluded as these are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses
that management does not consider part of ongoing operating results when assessing the performance of the Company&#146;s business, and also because the total amount of expense is partially outside of the Company&#146;s control as it is based on
factors such as stock price volatility and interest rates, which may be unrelated to our performance during the period in which the expense is incurred. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Amortization and Depreciation: Purchased assets and intangibles are amortized over a period of several years and
generally cannot be changed or influenced by management after they are acquired. Accordingly, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items are not considered by management in making operating decisions, and management believes that
such expenses do not have a direct correlation to future business operations. Thus, including such charges does not accurately reflect the performance of the Company&#146;s ongoing operations for the period in which such charges are incurred.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Litigation related: These expenses consist primarily of settlement, legal and other professional fees related to
litigation. The Company excludes these costs from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures primarily because the Company believes that these costs have no direct correlation to the core operations of the Company.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On occasion in the future, there may be other items, such as loss on extinguishment of debt, significant asset impairments,
restructuring charges or significant gains or losses from contingencies that the Company may exclude if it believes that doing so is consistent with the goal of providing useful information to investors and management. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Set forth below is a reconciliation of the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Adjusted EBITDA&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(In thousands except
for per share data) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="82%"></TD>
